class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-plp-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-plp-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-plp-c106="" class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>int32_t <span class="hljs-built_in">OH_ArkUI_RenderNodeUtils_AddRenderNode</span>(ArkUI_NodeHandle node, ArkUI_RenderNodeHandle child)</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>描述：</strong></p>     <p>向父自定义节点添加子渲染节点。</p>     <p></p>     <p>仅支持customNode类型的父节点。</p>     <p></p>     <p>每个自定义节点只能挂载一个ArkUI_RenderNodeHandle。</p>     <p></p>     <p>customNode无法挂载其他ArkUI_NodeHandle。</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 20</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow"> </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-arkui-nativemodule-arkui-node8h">ArkUI_NodeHandle</a> node</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">目标节点。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-arkui-nativemodule-arkui-rendernodehandle">ArkUI_RenderNodeHandle</a> child</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">目标渲染节点。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.15.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.6.15.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">int32_t</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>错误码。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-type-h#arkui_errorcode">ARKUI_ERROR_CODE_NO_ERROR</a> 成功。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-type-h#arkui_errorcode">ARKUI_ERROR_CODE_PARAM_INVALID</a> 函数参数异常。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-type-h#arkui_errorcode">ARKUI_ERROR_CODE_CAPI_INIT_ERROR</a> CAPI初始化失败。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-type-h#arkui_errorcode">ARKUI_ERROR_CODE_NOT_CUSTOM_NODE</a> 目标节点非自定义节点。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-type-h#arkui_errorcode">ARKUI_ERROR_CODE_CHILD_EXISTED</a> 目标节点已存在子节点。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-type-h#arkui_errorcode">ARKUI_ERROR_CODE_RENDER_PARENT_EXISTED</a> 目标渲染节点存在父节点。</p></td>        </tr> class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.7.1.3.1.1" width="50%">参数项</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-arkui-nativemodule-arkui-rendernodehandle">ArkUI_RenderNodeHandle</a> node</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">目标渲染节点。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">float* matrix</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">4x4 变换矩阵的浮点数数组（16 个连续值）。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p>变换矩阵应作为 16 个连续的浮点值以行优先顺序提供：</p>     <p>[m00, m01, m02, m03,</p>     <p>m10, m11, m12, m13,</p>     <p>m20, m21, m22, m23,</p>     <p>m30, m31, m32, m33]</p>     <p>其中矩阵表示为：</p>     <p>| m00 m01 m02 m03 |</p>     <p>| m10 m11 m12 m13 |</p>     <p>| m20 m21 m22 m23 |</p>     <p>| m30 m31 m32 m33 |</p>     <p>矩阵组件：</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.19.1.3.1.1" width="50%">矩阵单元</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.19.1.3.1.2" width="50%">描述</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m00</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">x轴的缩放值。单位矩阵的默认值为1。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m01</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">第二个值，受 x、y、z 轴的旋转或倾斜影响。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m02</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">第三个值，受 x、y、z 轴的旋转影响。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m03</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">第四个值，受透视投影影响。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m10</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">第五个值，受 x、y、z 轴的旋转或倾斜影响。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m11</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">y轴的缩放值。单位矩阵的默认值为1。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m12</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">第七个值，受 x、y、z 轴的旋转影响。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m13</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">第八个值，受透视投影影响。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m20</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">第九个值，受 x、y、z 轴的旋转影响。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m21</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">第十个值，受 x、y、z 轴的旋转影响。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m22</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">z轴的缩放值。单位矩阵的默认值为1。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m23</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">第 12 个值，受透视投影影响。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m30</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">x轴的平移值（以 px 为单位）。单位矩阵的默认值为0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m31</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">y轴的平移值（以 px 为单位）。单位矩阵的默认值为0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m32</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">z轴的平移值（以 px 为单位）。单位矩阵的默认值为0。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">m33</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">在齐次坐标中有效，呈现透视投影效果。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.21.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.42.21.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">int32_t</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">          <p>错误码。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-type-h#arkui_errorcode">ARKUI_ERROR_CODE_NO_ERROR</a> 成功。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-type-h#arkui_errorcode">ARKUI_ERROR_CODE_PARAM_INVALID</a> 函数参数异常。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-type-h#arkui_errorcode">ARKUI_ERROR_CODE_CAPI_INIT_ERROR</a> CAPI初始化失败。</p>          <p><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/capi-native-type-h#arkui_errorcode">ARKUI_ERROR_CODE_PARAM_OUT_OF_RANGE</a> 参数超出范围。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1015px;">     <h3 id="oh_arkui_rendernodeutils_setshadowcolor" class="screen prettyprint linenums hljs language-scss" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li>int32_t <span class="hljs-built_in">OH_ArkUI_RenderNodeUtils_SetMask</span>(ArkUI_RenderNodeHandle node, ArkUI_RenderNodeMaskOption* mask)</li></ol></pre></div></div>     <p><strong>描述：</strong></p>     <p>使用遮罩配置为渲染节点应用遮罩。</p>     <p>遮罩创建方式如下：</p>     <p>1.给遮罩图层增加亮度和线性颜色滤镜。</p>     <p>2.在该滤镜下绘制遮罩图形。</p>     <p>3.</p>     <p>将原节点图像作为源颜色，遮罩图形为目标颜色，通过<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-graphics-drawing-e#blendmode">BlendMode.SRC_IN</a>方式混合成Mask图像。</p>     <p><strong>起始版本：</strong> 20</p>  <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">目标渲染节点。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a width="50%">遮罩配置的指针。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table
